Test Shock Default (Risky + Safe Asset + Save + Borr + R Shock + Interpolated-Percentage), Test over Shock Mean and SD (cross)

back to Fan's Dynamic Assets Repository Table of Content. cross test: given (x,y), vary x along X, y along Y, one at a time

Compare against fsi_iwkz_ds_vecsv_shock_cross from iwkz. Here, we use ipwkz.

@include

  • ff_az_test_analyze
  • ffs_ipwkbzr_set_default_param

@seealso

  • test speed: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_speed_default
  • test joint RANDOM: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_joint_default_rand
  • test interest rate default: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_default
  • test interest rate default RANDOM: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_default_rand
  • test interest rate default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_default_cross
  • test interest rate no default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_nbc_cross
  • test preference default: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_pref_default
  • test preference default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_pref_default_cross
  • test preference no default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_pref_nbc_cross
  • test ymin and save r default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_price_default_cross
  • test ymin and save r no default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_price_nbc_cross
  • test preference default: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_prod_default
  • test production default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_prod_default_cross
  • test production no default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_prod_nbc_cross
  • test shock default: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_shk_default
  • test shock default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_shk_default_cross
  • test shock no default CROSS: fsi_ipwkbzr_ds_vecsv_shk_nbc_cross

Contents

  • Set Shared Parameters
  • Simulate and Graph
  • Quick Grid Simulation (Limited Graphs)
  • Medium Grid Simulation (Limited Graphs)
  • Larger Grid Simulation

Set Shared Parameters

% Borrowing/Savings Parameters
bl_default = true;

Simulate and Graph

% Set which to graph, simulate over which variables
bl_simu_cross = 'c';
cl_st_param_keys = {'fl_z_wage_rho', 'fl_z_wage_sig'};

% Generate Benchmark Parameters
it_param_set = 9;
[param_map, support_map] = ffs_ipwkbzr_set_default_param(it_param_set);

% Borrowing Parameters
param_map('bl_default') = bl_default;

% Support Parameters
support_map('bl_replacefile') = false;
support_map('bl_graph_onebyones') = true;
support_map('bl_display_graph_stats') = false;
support_map('st_mat_test_prefix') = ['dft_'];

% Generate Arrays of Parameter Values to Loop Over
it_simu_vec_len = 15;
param_tstar_map = containers.Map('KeyType','char', 'ValueType','any');
param_tstar_map('fl_z_wage_rho') = linspace(0, 0.985, it_simu_vec_len);
param_tstar_map('fl_z_wage_sig') = linspace(0.05, 0.65, it_simu_vec_len);

Quick Grid Simulation (Limited Graphs)

it_size_type = 1;
ar_it_plot_sets = [3,4,102, 104,105,106];

% Simulate along parameters
ff_az_test_analyze( ...
    ar_it_plot_sets, bl_simu_cross, it_size_type, cl_st_param_keys, ...
    param_map, support_map, param_tstar_map);

close all;
